about_this_resource_text: <p><strong>Description:</strong> This lecture introduced
  the concept of lifecycle management and also summarized other key concepts taught
  through the semester.</p> <p><strong>Instructor:</strong> Olivier de Weck</p>

  <span m='4480900'>Here,</span> <span m='4481670'>time,</span> <span m='4481990'>the</span>
  <span m='4482100'>15</span> <span m='4482490'>years,</span> <span m='4482790'>have</span>
  <span m='4482960'>been</span> <span m='4483360'>sub-divided</span> <span m='4483870'>into</span>
  <span m='4485010'>five</span> <span m='4485430'>three-year</span> <span m='4486330'>periods.</span>
  </p><p><span m='4487390'>So</span> <span m='4487440'>here's</span> <span m='4487620'>a</span>
  <span m='4487680'>sample</span> <span m='4488100'>scenario,</span> <span m='4488670'>demand</span>
  <span m='4489060'>goes</span> <span m='4489330'>up,</span> <span m='4489870'>goes</span>
  <span m='4490080'>up,</span> <span m='4490800'>and</span> <span m='4490920'>then</span>

  <span m='4495250'>discretized</span> <span m='4496050'>random</span> <span m='4496470'>walk.</span>

  <span m='4498180'>choose</span> <span m='4498840'>the</span> <span m='4498990'>numbers,</span>
